# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
because in between -1 and 0, x^3 is above x. 
When between 0, and 1, x is higher than x^3 ^uVFJ2cVa

If you were a nerd you could have used the fact that it is mirrored and just used one calculation
Apparently this will be a future complex unfamiliar question
